# <a name="removed-or-deprecated-features-in-previous-releases"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-103">先前版本中已删除或弃用的功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-103">Removed or deprecated features in previous releases</span></span>

[!include [banner](../includes/banner.md)]

[!include [rename-banner](~/includes/cc-data-platform-banner.md)]

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-104">此主题不再更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-104">This topic is no longer updated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-105">若要查看已经从 Finance and Operations 应用删除或弃用的功能的当前列表，请搜索与您在使用的应用有关的 **已删除或弃用的功能** 内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-105">To see a current list of features that have been removed or deprecated from Finance and Operations apps, search for **"Removed or deprecated features"** content that relates to the app you're using.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ca723-106">此主题介绍从 Dynamics 365 for Finance and Operations 和该产品的早期版本已经删除或弃用的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-106">This topic describes features that have been removed or deprecated from Dynamics 365 for Finance and Operations and previous releases of that product.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="ca723-107">*已移除* 的功能在产品中不再可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-107">A *removed* feature is no longer available in the product.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="ca723-108">*已弃用* 的功能在活跃的开发中不存在，而且在将来的更新中可能被移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-108">A *deprecated* feature is not in active development and may be removed in a future update.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ca723-109">此列表旨在帮助您在您自己的计划中考虑这些功能的移除和弃用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-109">This list is intended to help you consider these removals and deprecations for your own planning.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="ca723-110">[技术参考报告](https://docs.microsoft.com/dynamics/s-e/global/axtechrefrep_61)中提供了有关 Finance and Operations应用中的对象的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-110">Detailed information about objects in Finance and Operations apps can be found in the [Technical reference reports](https://docs.microsoft.com/dynamics/s-e/global/axtechrefrep_61).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-111">可比较这些报告的不同版本，以了解 Finance and Operations 应用各版本中已更改或已删除的对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-111">You can compare the different versions of these reports to learn about objects that have changed or been removed in each version of Finance and Operations apps.</span></span>

### <a name="data-management-staging-clean-up"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-197">清除数据管理暂存</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-197">Data management staging clean up</span></span>
|&nbsp;   | &nbsp; |
|------------|--------------------|

#### <a name="deriving-from-internal-classes-is-deprecated"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-291">已弃用从内部类派生</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-291">Deriving from internal classes is deprecated</span></span>

| &nbsp;  |&nbsp;  |
|------------|--------------------|

<span data-ttu-id="ca723-337">客户可使用嵌入的 SQL Server Reporting Services (SSRS) ReportViewer 控件提供的 **导出** 操作下载 Finance and Operations 应用程序生成的单据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-337">Customers can use the **Export** action provided by the embedded SQL Server Reporting Services (SSRS) ReportViewer control to download documents produced by Finance and Operations applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-338">这种基于 HTML 的报表表示为用户提供不分页的单据预览。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-338">This HTML-based presentation of the report offers users a non-paginated preview of the document.</span></span>

### <a name="deprecated-apis-and-future-breaking-changes"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-364">已弃用的 API 和将来的突破性更改</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-364">Deprecated APIs and future breaking changes</span></span>

#### <a name="field-groups-containing-invalid-field-references"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-365">其中包含无效字段引用的字段组</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-365">Field groups containing invalid field references</span></span>

| &nbsp;  |&nbsp;  |
|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-366">**弃用/移除的原因**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-366">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-367">表元数据定义中可以有包含无效字段引用的字段组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-367">It is possible for table metadata definitions to have field groups containing invalid field references.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-368">如果部署，可能导致 Financial Reporting 和 SQL Server Reporting Services (SSRS) 中发生运行时失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-368">If deployed, this can cause runtime failures in Financial Reporting and SQL Server Reporting Services (SSRS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-369">此问题目前归类为 *编译器警告*，而不是 *错误*，这意味着可以在不解决此问题的情况下继续创建和部署可部署包。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-369">This issue is currently categorized as a *compiler warning* rather than an *error*, meaning that the deployable package creation and deployment can proceed without fixing the issue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-370">要解决此问题，请执行以下操作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-370">To fix this issue:</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="ca723-371">1. 删除表字段组定义中的无效字段引用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-371">1. Remove the invalid field reference from the table field group definition.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="ca723-372">2. 重新编译。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-372">2. Recompile.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="ca723-373">3. 确保解决所有警告或错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-373">3. Ensure any warnings or errors are addressed.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-374">**被另一个功能取代？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-374">**Replaced by another feature?**</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-375">以后此警告将替换为编译器错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-375">This warning will be replaced by a compile error in the future.</span></span> |

## <a name="finance-and-operations-81-with-platform-update-20"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-384">带平台更新 20 的 Finance and Operations 8.1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-384">Finance and Operations 8.1 with Platform update 20</span></span>

### <a name="batch-transfer-rules-for-subledger-journal-account-entries"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-385">子分类日记帐科目分录的批处理转移规则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-385">Batch transfer rules for subledger journal account entries</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ca723-386">总帐参数中已弃用了同步转移模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-386">The Synchronous transfer mode is being deprecated in the General ledger parameters.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="ca723-387">此模式刚被异步和计划批处理，后者表示为转移选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-387">This mode is replaced by Asynchronous and scheduled batch only, which already exist as options for transfer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-388">有关更多信息，请参阅[总帐参数 – 批量转移规则](https://community.dynamics.com/365/financeandoperations/b/financials/archive/2019/03/15/general-ledger-parameters-batch-transfer-rules)博客。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-388">For additional information, see the [General Ledger Parameters – Batch transfer rules](https://community.dynamics.com/365/financeandoperations/b/financials/archive/2019/03/15/general-ledger-parameters-batch-transfer-rules) blog.</span></span>

### <a name="personalized-product-recommendations"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-455">个性化产品建议</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-455">Personalized product recommendations</span></span> 
<span data-ttu-id="ca723-456">从 2018 年 2 月 15 日开始，零售商再也不能显示有关销售点 (POS) 设备的个性化产品建议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-456">Starting February 15, 2018, retailers will no longer be able to display personalized product recommendations on a point of sale (POS) device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-457">有关详细信息，请参阅[产品建议概览](../../../commerce/product-recommendations.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-457">For more information, see [Product recommendations overview](../../../commerce/product-recommendations.md).</span></span>

### <a name="extension-of-the-list-of-electronic-reporting-er-functions"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-470">电子申报 (ER) 功能列表扩展</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-470">Extension of the list of Electronic reporting (ER) functions</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ca723-471">可以引入在 ER 表达式生成器中使用的自定义功能（有关详细信息，请参阅[扩展电子申报 (ER) 功能列表](../../dev-itpro/analytics/general-electronic-reporting-formulas-list-extension.md)）的这一特性不再受支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-471">The possibility to introduce custom functions to be used in the ER expression builder (for more information, see [Extend the list of Electronic reporting (ER) functions](../../dev-itpro/analytics/general-electronic-reporting-formulas-list-extension.md)) is not supported any more.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-472">由于 ER API 发生变更，从 ER 表达式生成器调用内置函数的 API 变成内部 API，并且无法再进行扩展。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-472">Due to changes of the ER APIs, the API to call built-in functions from the ER expression builder became internal and can’t be extended any longer.</span></span>

| &nbsp;  | &nbsp; |
|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-473">**弃用/移除的原因**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-473">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-474">代码密封计划</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-474">Code sealing initiative</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-475">**被另一个功能取代？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-475">**Replaced by another feature?**</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-476">无。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-476">None.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-477">每当需要一个新的内置函数时，必须向 ER 框架团队提交新扩展请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-477">Whenever a new built-in function is needed, a new extension request must be addressed to the ER framework team.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="ca723-478">在 ER 团队开发请求的函数时，作为临时解决方案，可以将需要的逻辑作为一种自定义应用程序类方法进行编程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-478">As a temporary work around while the requested function is under development by the ER team, the required logic can be programmed as a method of a custom application class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-479">此方法可以作为引用该自定义应用程序类的 **应用程序\类** 类型的已添加 ER 数据源的属性在 ER 表达式中访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-479">This method can be accessed in an ER expression as a property of the added ER data source of the **Application\Class** type that refers to that custom application class.</span></span>  |

## <a name="dynamics-365-for-retail-72"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-574">Dynamics 365 for Retail 7.2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-574">Dynamics 365 for Retail 7.2</span></span>

### <a name="personalized-product-recommendations"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-575">个性化产品建议</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-575">Personalized product recommendations</span></span> 
<span data-ttu-id="ca723-576">从 2018 年 2 月 15 日开始，零售商再也不能显示有关销售点 (POS) 设备的个性化产品建议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-576">Starting February 15, 2018, retailers will no longer be able to display personalized product recommendations on a point of sale (POS) device.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-577">有关详细信息，请参阅[产品建议概览](../../../commerce/product-recommendations.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-577">For more information, see [Product recommendations overview](../../../commerce/product-recommendations.md).</span></span>  

|  &nbsp; |  &nbsp;|
|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-578">**弃用/移除的原因**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-578">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-579">我们将移除当前的产品建议服务版本，因为我们为这项功能重新设计了更出色的算法和更新的面向零售的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-579">We are removing the current version of the product recommendation service as we redesign this feature with a better algorithm and newer retail-oriented capabilities.</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-580">**被另一个功能取代？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-580">**Replaced by another feature?**</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-581">编号</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-581">No.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-582">但是，我们计划在 2018 年春季之后恢复此功能，以利用新的建议服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-582">However, after Spring 2018, we plan to bring back this feature to leverage a new recommendation service.</span></span>   |

### <a name="modifications-in-the-chart-of-accounts-and-accounting-rules-for-spain"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-784">修改西班牙的会计科目表和会计规则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-784">Modifications in the chart of accounts and accounting rules for Spain</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ca723-785">此功能用于修改西班牙的会计科目表和会计规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-785">This feature is used for changes in the chart of accounts and accounting rules in Spain.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-786">它映射帐户，以帮助将旧的会计科目表转换到新的会计科目表，将上一个会计年度与新的会计年度相比较，即使是当它们过帐到不同的科目编号时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-786">It maps accounts to help transform the old chart of accounts into the new chart of accounts, and compares the previous fiscal year with the new fiscal year, even if they were posted to different account numbers.</span></span>

### <a name="aif-axd-and-axbc-integrations"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-973">AIF、Axd 和 AxBC 集成</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-973">AIF, AxD, and AxBC integrations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ca723-974">在应用集成框架 (AIF) 中，数据可以通过显示为服务的业务逻辑与外部系统交换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-974">In Application Integration Framework (AIF), data can be exchanged with external systems through business logic that is exposed as services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-975">Dynamics AX 包括基于文档和 .NET Business Connector (AxBC) 的服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-975">Dynamics AX includes services that are based on documents and .NET Business Connector (AxBC).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-976">文档是通过使用 XML 创建的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-976">A document is created by using XML.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-977">XML 包括标题信息，添加该信息的目的是创建可在 Dynamics AX 内外传送的 *消息*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-977">The XML includes header information that is added to create a *message* that can be transferred into or out of Dynamics AX.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-978">文档的示例包括销售订单和采购订单。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-978">Examples of documents include sales orders and purchase orders.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-979">但是，几乎所有实体（例如客户）都可以被文档代表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-979">However, almost any entity, such as a customer, can be represented by a document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-980">基于文档的服务使用 **Axd \<Document\>** 类。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-980">Services that are based on documents use the **Axd \<Document\>** classes.</span></span>

### <a name="data-partitions"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-1146">数据分区</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1146">Data partitions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ca723-1147">数据分区在 Dynamics AX 数据库中提供数据的逻辑界定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1147">Data partitions provide a logical separation of data in the Dynamics AX database.</span></span>

| &nbsp;  | &nbsp; |
|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1148">**弃用/移除的原因**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1148">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1149">数据分区在 Dynamics AX 2012 R2 引入以启用数据隔离。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1149">Data partitions were introduced in Dynamics AX 2012 R2 to enable data isolation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1150">在常见情况中，公司有子公司，一个子公司的数据不应对另一个子公司可见，即使两个子公司均由相同的 IT 部门管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1150">In a common scenario, a company has subsidiaries, and the data from one subsidiary should not be visible to another subsidiary, even though both subsidiaries are managed by the same IT department.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1151">不过，整个程序都需要额外的脚本和管理开销来创建新的分区并填充数据，以及备份分区数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1151">However, extra scripts and management overhead throughout the program were required in order to create new partitions and populate them with data, and to back up partition data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1152">在云中，在其中我们有访问平台即服务 (PaaS) 数据库服务（Microsoft Azure SQL 数据库）的权限，则使用数据库作为隔离容器比在程序中执行隔离要高效得多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1152">In the cloud, where we have access to platform as a service (PaaS) database services (Microsoft Azure SQL Database), it's much more efficient to use a database as the isolation container than to do isolation in the program.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1153">不管是子公司、多个租户，或只为规模需要进行数据分区，我们认为通过多个 Finance and Operations 实例都可以更好地处理这种情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1153">Regardless of whether data partitioning is required for subsidiaries, for multiple tenants, or just for scale, we believe that the scenarios can be handled better through multiple instances of Finance and Operations.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1154">**被另一个功能取代？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1154">**Replaced by another feature?**</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1155">如果数据库级别分隔是关键问题，使用数据分区的客户必须使用多个 Finance and Operations 实例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1155">Customers using data partitions must use multiple instances of Finance and Operations if database level separation is a critical issue.</span></span>    |
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1156">**影响的产品区域**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1156">**Product areas affected**</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1157">所有模块</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1157">All modules</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1158">**状态**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1158">**Status**</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1159">从 Dynamics AX 7.0 开始移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1159">Removed as of Dynamics AX 7.0.</span></span>  |


### <a name="database-and-file-share-storage-for-attachments"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-1160">数据库和文件共享附件存储</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1160">Database and file share storage for attachments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ca723-1161">Dynamics AX 2012 允许在数据库和文件共享中存储附件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1161">Dynamics AX 2012 allowed storage of attachments in the database and in file shares.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1162">这两个选项都不再受支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1162">Both of those options are no longer supported.</span></span>

| &nbsp;  | &nbsp; |
|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1163">**弃用/移除的原因**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1163">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1164">云托管的环境无法再与本地文件共享通信，因此文件共享存储不再受支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1164">Files share storage is no longer supported because cloud-hosted environments cannot communicate with local file shares.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1165">为了支持 Azure Blob 存储，数据库存储已弃用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1165">Database storage has been deprecated in favor of Azure Blob storage.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1166">Azure Blob 存储相当于数据库中的存储，因为文档仅可以通过 Finance and Operations 客户端窗体进行访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1166">Azure Blob storage is equivalent to storage in the database, as documents can only be accessed through Finance and Operations client forms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1167">这提供额外好处，即提供存储不会对数据库的性能造成不利影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1167">This provides the added benefit of providing storage that doesn't negatively affect the performance of the database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1168">Blob 存储是文档管理的默认存储机制并立即生效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1168">Blob storage is the default storage mechanism for Document Management and works immediately.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1169">**被另一个功能取代？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1169">**Replaced by another feature?**</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1170">为了支持 Azure Blob 存储，数据库存储已弃用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1170">Database storage has been deprecated in favor of Azure Blob storage.</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1171">**影响的产品区域**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1171">**Product areas affected**</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1172">所有模块</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1172">All modules</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1173">**状态**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1173">**Status**</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1174">从 Dynamics AX 7.0 开始移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1174">Removed as of Dynamics AX 7.0.</span></span>   |

### <a name="desktop-client"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-1184">桌面客户端</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1184">Desktop client</span></span>

| &nbsp;  | &nbsp; |
|------------|--------------------|

### <a name="direct-database-connection"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-1193">直接数据库连接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1193">Direct database connection</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ca723-1194">在 Dynamics AX 2012 R3 中，Retail Modern POS 可以直接连接到与 Enterprise POS 方式相似的通道 DB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1194">In Dynamics AX 2012 R3, Retail Modern POS could connect directly to the Channel DB in similar fashion to Enterprise POS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1195">这是除通过 Retail Server 的 Retail Modern POS 通信的标准通信方法以外的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1195">This was in addition to the standard communication method of Retail Modern POS communicating through Retail Server.</span></span>

### <a name="product-builder"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-1383">产品生成器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1383">Product builder</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ca723-1384">产品生成器用于从销售订单、采购订单、生产订单、销售报价单、项目报价单或物料需求动态配置物料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1384">Product builder was used to dynamically configure items from a sales order, purchase order, production order, sales quotation, project quotation, or item requirement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1385">基于具有建模变量的产品模型，用户可以选择值以满足用户需求并获取具有物料清单和工艺路线的唯一产品变型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1385">Based on a product model that had modeling variables, the user could select values to meet the customer requirements and get a unique product variant that had a BOM and route.</span></span>

| &nbsp;  | &nbsp; |
|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1386">**弃用/移除的原因**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1386">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1387">产品生成器向最终用户显示了 X++ 代码，在 Dynamics AX 的当前版本中不受支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1387">Product builder exposed X++ code to end users and isn't supported in the current version of Dynamics AX.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1388">它已被删除，从而避免在重叠的、庞大的代码库中进行重复的维护工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1388">It has been removed to avoid duplicate maintenance efforts on overlapping, sizeable codebases.</span></span>  |

### <a name="virtual-company-accounts"></a><span data-ttu-id="ca723-1481">虚拟公司帐户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1481">Virtual company accounts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ca723-1482">Dynamics AX 中不再支持虚拟公司功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1482">The virtual companies feature is no longer supported in Dynamics AX.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1483">虚拟公司功能允许用户设置可以由一组公司共享的表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1483">The virtual companies feature let users set up tables that could be shared by a set of companies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1484">有关该功能的描述，请参阅[公司帐户和虚拟公司帐户](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/aa834382(v=ax.10).aspx)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1484">For a description of the feature, see [Company accounts and Virtual company accounts](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/aa834382(v=ax.10).aspx).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1485">该功能的工作原理是将表分组到集合，然后集合分配给虚拟公司，即现有的“实际”公司的组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1485">The feature works by grouping tables into collections that are assigned to virtual companies, which are groups of existing “real” companies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1486">创建查询，以便虚拟公司中的所有公司可以访问关联表集合的表中的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1486">Queries are created so that all the companies in the virtual company can access the data in the tables of the associated table collections.</span></span>

| &nbsp;  | &nbsp; |
|------------|--------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1487">**弃用/移除的原因**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1487">**Reason for deprecation/removal**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1488">- 将数据存储在表中之前，必须先设置虚拟公司。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1488">- Virtual companies must be set up before data is stored in the tables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1489">将虚拟公司更新到现有实施上是很困难的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1489">Retrofitting virtual companies onto an existing implementation is very difficult.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="ca723-1490">- 由于 Dynamics AX 的当前版本中有如此多数据标准化，要了解将什么添加到表集合将会很困难。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1490">- Because there has been so much data normalization in the current version of Dynamics AX, it has become difficult to know what to add to the table collections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1491">例如，要知道共享哪些表很难。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1491">For example, it's difficult to know which tables to share.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1492">还必须添加从虚拟公司中的表引用的所有表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1492">All the tables referenced from tables that are in a virtual company must also added.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1493">由于表标准化，即使遍布许多表中的简单主数据也必须是虚拟公司的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1493">Because of table normalization, even simple master data that is spread across multiple tables must be part of the virtual company.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1494">此处所犯的任何错误都将导致功能问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1494">Any mistake that is made here will cause functional issues.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="ca723-1495">- 当表是虚拟公司的一部分时，它会丢失有关数据来源的信息，并且只记录虚拟公司。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1495">- When a table is part of a virtual company, it loses information about the origin of the data, and only the virtual company is recorded.</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1496">**被另一个功能取代？**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1496">**Replaced by another feature?**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1497">全局表可用于使表可从所有公司访问到。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1497">Global tables can be used to make tables accessible from all companies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1498">当前不替换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1498">Currently, there is no replacement.</span></span> |   
| <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1499">**影响的产品区域**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1499">**Product areas affected**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="ca723-1500">所有模块</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ca723-1500">All modules</span></span> |
